g: a software program capable of reproducing itself that can spread from one computer to the next over a network; "worms take advantage of automatic file sending and receiving features found on many computers"

w: <<virus>>
w: <<computer_virus>>
hyper: [[malevolent_program]]
g: a software program capable of reproducing itself and usually capable of causing great harm to files or other programs on the same computer; "a true virus cannot spread to another computer without human assistance"

w: <<trojan>>
w: <<trojan_horse>>
hyper: [[malevolent_program]]
g: a program that appears desirable but actually contains something harmful; "the contents of a trojan can be a virus or a worm"; "when he downloaded the free game it turned out to be a trojan horse"

w: <<logic_bomb>>
w: <<slag_code>>
hyper: [[malevolent_program]]
g: a set of instructions inserted into a program that are designed to execute (or `explode') if a particular condition is satisfied; when exploded it may delete or corrupt data, or print a spurious message, or have other harmful effects; "a disgruntled employee planted a logic bomb"
